Spec `.ai/specs/agency-onboarding-feature-switchboard.md`; no migration. _Prior:_ **P24 "IMPORT ALL" REBUILT PARALLEL + LOSSLESS ‚Äî the old one silently shipped ~11% of galleries short (branch `QA2`, 10/10 green, NOT deployed).** The first go-live lost 2,549 of 23,124 images because 8 tabs √ó a 10-wide pool ‚âà 80 concurrent tripped P24's rate limiter and `DownloadP24RowImagesJob` (`tries=1`) swallowed the failures and wrote short galleries as "done". Now a **two-lane queue**: `p24import` WIDE (8 workers, DB writes, the speed) + `p24images` NARROW (4 workers ‚âà 40 concurrent, under the ~80 that caused loss). Confirm no longer downloads inline; the image job is **self-healing** (tries=5, fetch-only-missing, rebuild-from-disk, `release` while short, **can never report `complete` while short**). New `properties` gallery columns + owner `/api/v1/importer/gallery-reconciliation` prove "zero short". Import All is one `Bus::batch` click with a dual progress bar. **The real Import All is the public PORTAL, not the admin page.** **Workers are half the feature ‚Äî `docs/infra/supervisor/corex-worker-p24.conf` MUST be applied or jobs strand; QA sites have no worker ‚Üí first QA on Staging.** Forward-only (no backfill of the lost 11%). See ¬ß14 of `.ai/specs/importer.md` + ¬ß4 top. **The audit `.ai/audits/p24-import-throughput-live-2026-07-17.md` was written on the server and is NOT in git ‚Äî commit it.** _Prior:_ **P24 AGENT INVITES MOVED TO THE LAST STEP ‚Äî AND THE REVIEW PAGE WAS ALREADY BROKEN FOR ANY OWNER USING THE AGENCY SWITCHER (branch `QA2`, 13/13 green, NOT deployed).** Invites were sent from the agent **run detail** page mid-import, so an agent could be invited into a CoreX with **no properties in it** ‚Äî the first impression we get exactly once. They now go out per-agency from **Property Onboarding** (`admin.importer.review`), whose cards only exist once an agency has listings, so "properties first" is structural rather than a rule someone remembers. Scope is the **agency, not the run** (an agency imported over two runs is one agency to the person pressing the button). **The move forced two latent defects into the open.** (1) **Nothing recorded that an invite was ever sent** ‚Äî no column, anywhere ‚Äî so a bulk button would re-mail the whole agency on a second press; new `users.invited_at`, stamped inside `SendAgentInviteJob` **after** the notification is handed off (never at dispatch: a failed send must not mark an agent invited), which is the single choke point both paths share so they cannot drift. (2) **`sendAllInvites` sent every email synchronously inside the HTTP request** ‚Äî survivable as a per-run trickle, a guaranteed timeout as a 40-agent one-press; now `dispatch()` with an explicit `$timeout` on the job, the omission that SIGKILLed `SyncAgentToP24Job`. **The bug found on the way in is the one worth remembering: the review page has always been silently broken for an owner who uses the agency switcher.** `User`/`P24ImportRun`/`P24OnboardingPortal`/`P24PortalEvent` are all tenant-scoped, and AgencyScope no-ops for an owner **only** while `session('active_agency_id')` is unset ‚Äî set it, and every query returns empty and the page reports "no agents" for an agency with twenty, **with no error to explain it**. Fixed the class (every cross-agency query drops the scope explicitly) and pinned it with a regression test, rather than only the new code. Also: `users.email` is **NOT NULL + UNIQUE**, so the only representable "no email" is `''` ‚Äî the guard tests `blank()`, and the test that proved it initially failed by asserting a null the schema forbids. **Consequence to plan around: invites are queued, and QA sites have no worker ‚Äî this gets its first real QA on Staging, not qa1/qa2.** Local MySQL note: **XAMPP's MariaDB InnoDB tablespace is corrupt** (LSN-in-the-future, 2026-07-15) and will not start; **Laragon MySQL 8.4.3 is the live local DB** and holds `hfc_dash`/`hfc_dash_test`. _Prior:_ **AT-11 ‚Äî COREX HAS BEEN CHARGING AGENCIES MONEY THE PRODUCT COULD NOT NAME. Built the money model + both pages; 51 tests / 134 assertions green on `AT-11-Payment-gate-for-payments`, NOT deployed.** No price, no plan, no seat count existed anywhere in the schema. Now: agency-facing read-only `/corex/billing` (what you owe **and the itemised arithmetic**, so an agency can check our maths) + owner-only `/corex/admin/billing` (every agency, with custom-amount / discount controls). Team = headcount √ó R450 (‚â§10); Agency = R1 495 base + **graduated** tiers (295/250/195) ‚Äî **25 users = R7 920**, asserted verbatim, because a flat 25√óR195 is R6 370 and nobody would catch a R1 550/mo error until an agency queried an invoice. Extra branches R750, first free, **both plans** (the plans are price shapes, not feature sets ‚Äî Johan). No VAT. **A seat is ANY active user** (a login is a seat); **the count is read LIVE and never stored**, so the bill cannot go stale no matter what changed a user ‚Äî events + the nightly sweep exist only to make the plan-change **email** prompt, never to keep the **number** right. The flip is a **compare-and-set** (one email per switch, never two); the discount **expires by arithmetic** (no cron can forget it); custom-vs-discount is guarded three deep. Owner page is `owner_only` with **no permission key on purpose** ‚Äî a key is grantable, and one mis-click shows an agency admin every competitor's rate. **Phase 2 (the actual cutoff/lockout) deliberately NOT built** ‚Äî specced to reuse `maintenance_mode`; you cannot gate on money the system can't yet name. **Needs Johan: spec sign-off + confirm nothing belongs in the onboarding wizard (¬ß14).** _Prior:_ **MIXED-CASE COLUMNS ARE ADVERTISING THE WRONG THING ‚Äî a rental "For Sale" (94 listings) AND a SOLD property "For Sale" (60 listings). LIVE `/corex` + Staging; hotfixes `dee61c28` + `de1c10bd`.** Two fixes, one root cause, found one after the other. **(1)** Property 6075 ("‚Ä¶to let in Uvongo") showed a **For Sale** badge on its live preview ‚Äî the blade hardcoded `'active' => 'For Sale'` and never consulted `listing_type`, so **every** active rental was advertised for sale; the price card said "Asking price" over a monthly rent and a **bond calculator** costed a bond on R13,900. `Property::isRental()` is now THE predicate (case-insensitive, whole vocabulary ‚Äî the P24 CSV importer writes a capitalised `'Rental'` that every case-sensitive check missed). **(2)** Verifying (1) on staging surfaced the worse twin: **`properties.status` is mixed-case too** ('Active' 444 rows, 'Sold' **60**, 'Rented' 1 ‚Äî the P24 sync capitalises), and every badge compared it case-sensitively, so **60 SOLD properties were badged "For Sale" on the pickers and "FOR SALE" on generated ad cards**, a tenanted property advertised "TO LET", and 1,703 listings fell through the preview's badge map to a raw DB value shown to clients ("Let_out", "Under_offer"). `Property::normalizedStatus()` is now THE way to read status; `statusBadge()`, `adData()` and the preview badge all route through it; `rented`/`let_out` finally count as concluded (the rental "sold"). `pending` deliberately keeps its own badge (Johan's call). Verified on live across every stored casing. **RULE, now twice-proven: a CoreX enum column is not normalised on write ‚Äî never compare one case-sensitively; go through the model's canonical reader.** **Tests not run ‚Äî no dev deps on the server; `dev-check.ps1` owes `PropertyLivePreviewListingTypeTest` a run on Windows.**
> _Prior:_ 2026-07-14 by **A RENTAL WAS ADVERTISED "FOR SALE" ON THE LIVE PREVIEW ‚Äî 94 LIVE LISTINGS, NOT ONE (LIVE `/corex`, hotfix on main `dee61c28`).** Reported on property 6075 ("‚Ä¶to let in Uvongo"). The preview blade mapped status‚Üíbadge with a hardcoded `'active' => 'For Sale'` and **never consulted `listing_type` at all**, so every active rental was advertised for sale on the page an agent sends to a client. Two more sale-assumptions sat on the same page: the price card read **"Asking price"** over a monthly rent, and a **bond calculator** offered the tenant a repayment schedule on a purchase that will never happen (on 6075 it costed a bond on R13,900). **The class under the instance:** "is this a rental?" was answered inline in **six places with divergent vocabularies and case-sensitive comparisons** ‚Äî `statusBadge()`/`adData()` took `rental|to_let`, `effectivePrice()` lowercased but took only `rental`, the P24/PP deep-link builders took only lowercase `rental`, two blades rolled their own, the website API took `rental|to_let|to-let|lease` ‚Äî **while `P24ListingsCsvParser` writes a capitalised `'Rental'`**, which every one of those checks would have missed. **`Property::isRental()` is now THE predicate** (case-insensitive, whole vocabulary, one place); every check routes through it. The case-tolerance is **preventive** ‚Äî no row carries the capitalised spelling today, but the importer that writes it is live. Verified by rendering the real view for 6075: badge **To Let**, **Monthly rental R 13 900 / month**, no calculator; the sale control still reads For Sale / Asking price and keeps its calculator; confirmed on the live URL after php8.4-fpm reload. **The preview page had no test at all ‚Äî which is how it shipped**; `PropertyLivePreviewListingTypeTest` now pins the badge, the price label, the calculator's absence, dead-status precedence, and the full vocabulary incl. the importer casing. **Tests not run on the server ‚Äî no dev deps there; `dev-check.ps1` owes them a run on Windows.**

> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **PP-B3 RESOLVED ‚Äî 5 attributes were emitted in the WRONG PP Appendix A datatype ‚Üí LIVE `main` + Staging**. The audit's highest-priority open item (potential PP106 whole-listing rejection) was settled with a **read-only `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` call against the live HFC branch (327 listings)** ‚Äî the authoritative datatype ground truth. Result: `Kitchen`(191/191 stored `"Yes"`), `Family_TV_Room`(11), `Study`(13), `StaffQuarters`(16), `Entrance_hall`(37) are all **boolean `"Yes"`** in Appendix A, but `PrivatePropertyListingMapper::buildAttributes()` emitted them as **integer counts** in the `$counts` loop ‚Äî a datatype mismatch. **Why it never visibly broke:** PP *coerces* a numeric value to `"Yes"` for boolean attributes (the ONLY reason property 6049 survived with `Kitchen="1"` ‚Äî the audit's "Kitchen is a proven count" anchor was WRONG; PP silently coerced it). The 2026-07-02 PP106s were the *reverse* mismatch (old `EnSuite="true"` boolean ‚Üí integer attr, since fixed to `EnSuite="1"`). **Fix:** the five moved out of `$counts` into present-only `"Yes"` flags (keyed off `Kitchen`/`TV Room`/`Study`+`Office`/`Domestic Room`/`Entrance Hall` spaces); `Lounges`/`DiningAreas`/`Parking`/`Carports` stay integer counts (read-back-confirmed 1‚Äì3). Tinker-verified: buildAttributes now emits Kitchen/Family_TV_Room/Study/StaffQuarters/Entrance_hall=`"Yes"`, Lounges/DiningAreas/Parking/Carports=int. `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` is the standard read-back to settle any future count-vs-flag question (WSDL op exists; called via the client's generic `call()`). Files: `PrivatePropertyListingMapper.php`, audit doc (PP-B3 ‚Üí RESOLVED). No migration/route/perm. ‚öÝÔ∏è live box is `--no-dev` ‚Üí run `PpFeatureAttributesTest` on laragon.

> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **SYNDICATION MAPPING FIXES (5) ‚Üí LIVE `main` + Staging**. From the 2026-07-05 syndication-mapping audit (`.ai/audits/syndication-mapping-audit-2026-07-05.md`), the five confirmed "fix-now" items landed. **PP (`PrivatePropertyListingMapper`):** (PP-B1) `Carports` was dead code ‚Äî `countSpaces($property,'Carport')` but a carport is a FEATURE of the `Parking` space, not a space type, so it always returned 0 and never syndicated ‚Üí new `countCarports()` sums Parking bays/units carrying the `Carport` feature (space-level featuresAll ‚áí bay count, else per-unit hits; tinker-proven 2/2/0). (PP-G1) seven amenity flags (Gym/Clubhouse/TennisCourt/SquashCourt/Jaccuzzi/Jetty_Berth/Storage) only checked `has()` feature strings, so entered as a SPACE they never fired ‚Üí OR-ed the matching `hasSpace(<type>)` (Gym/Clubhouse/Tennis Court/Squash Court/Jacuzzi/Jetty/Storeroom, all verified against `config/property-spaces.php`). **P24 (`Property24ListingMapper`):** (P24-B1) `showLocation` used `(bool)($lat && $lng)` but lat/lng are `decimal:7` string casts ("0.0000000" is truthy) ‚Üí never-geocoded listings emitted `showLocation:true` (privacy-adjacent) ‚Üí numeric guard mirroring the proven line-82 `geographicLocation` fix. (P24-G1) `rentalInfo.rentalRate` never sent ‚Üí weekly/daily/short-term rentals published at P24's default MONTHLY cadence ‚Üí new `mapRentalRate()` maps `rental_price_type` ‚Üí RentalRate enum (Month/Week/Day/Year/SquareMetre), NULL for blank/unknown so P24 keeps its own default. ‚öÝÔ∏è LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit) ‚Üí verification was `php -l`-clean + a bootstrapped tinker harness (Carports both shapes, all 8 space strings resolve, every rental cadence maps); the covering test files (`tests/Unit/PrivateProperty/PpFeatureAttributesTest.php`, `tests/Unit/Syndication/Property24FeatureTagsTest.php`) must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`. > _Prior:_ 2026-07-04 by **P24 SUBMIT-TIMEOUT HOTFIX ‚Äî a transient Property24 timeout no longer clobbers a LIVE listing to 'error' ‚Üí LIVE `main`**. Symptom (Johan): property **1357** (ref **117201765**) showed `P24 Ref: 117201765 ‚Äî Error  Error: Connection failed: cURL error 28: Operation timed out after 120000ms with 0 bytes received` ‚Äî a listing that was STILL LIVE on the portal, mislabelled broken; **5 submit timeouts on 2026-07-04** (P24-side slowness ‚Äî 0 bytes back within the 120s read timeout; today also 16 connect-timeouts on harmless `status_check`). ROOT CAUSE: `Property24SyndicationService::performSubmit()` wrote a permanent `p24_syndication_status='error'` + the raw cURL string into `p24_last_error` on ANY save failure ‚Äî INCLUDING a transient timeout (no HTTP status). The `isTransientFailure()` classifier already existed and was correctly used by `deactivate/reactivate` (AT-P24 #5) but **never by the submit/update path**. An `error` row additionally (a) lost every UI recovery button (View/Refresh/Deactivate require active|submitted|submitting) and (b) was excluded from `syncAllActivations()` reconcile ‚Üí **stranded**. FIX (root-cause, mirrors AT-P24 #5): `performSubmit` now branches transient‚Üí`handleTransientSubmitFailure()` ‚Äî **has p24_ref ‚Üí keep 'active'** (it's still live) + amber "Sync deferred ‚Äî still live; tap Refresh to retry" note; **no ref ‚Üí 'pending'** (retryable), never a hard error. Permanent 4xx (validation) ‚Üí unchanged crimson `error`. UI (`properties/show.blade.php`): sync-state poller no longer shows a FALSE "success" toast when a deferred note is present, and a new amber status line surfaces the note on reload (buttons stay). REMEDIATION: property 1357 verified live via a real `isOnPortal` call (`data:true`) ‚Üí reset to `active`/enabled, error cleared. TEST: `tests/Feature/Syndication/Property24SubmitTransientFailureTest.php` (2 cases: live-listing timeout stays active / first-submit timeout ‚Üí pending). ‚öÝÔ∏è the LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit/collision) ‚Üí this test must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`; here it was `php -l`-clean and the transient classification tinker-verified (timeout/503‚Üítransient, 422‚Üípermanent). Files: `Property24SyndicationService.php`, `resources/views/corex/properties/show.blade.php`, new test. No migration, no new route/perm.

> _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-106 ‚Äî daily self-cleaning P24 location sync (stamp-and-sweep) ‚Üí LIVE (direct to main)**. Answers "how do we keep provinces/cities/suburbs always correct so a phantom can't recur": `p24:sync-locations` now **stamps `p24_verified_at=now()` on every province/city/suburb P24 returns**, then **soft-deletes anything it did NOT return this run** (verified_at < runStart) ‚Äî and is **scheduled daily at 11:00** (`routes/console.php`, `withoutOverlapping`; the old monthly entry removed as redundant). This makes the tree self-healing: removed P24 locations (the city-tier staleness AT-105 found ‚Äî Durban North/785 etc.) get swept automatically; new ones appear. **Safety:** the full walk aborts on ANY fetch error before pruning, AND an **absolute sanity floor** (P24 must return ‚â• 5 provinces / 50 cities / 3000 suburbs) skips the sweep on a truncated/auth-broken reply so an API blip can never wipe the tree (deliberately absolute, NOT a ratio-of-current-table ‚Äî the table is bloated with stale rows the first sweep must clear). Pruned suburbs remediate dependent properties (FK chain nulled + `p24_suburb_mismatch=1`); pruned cities/provinces null the matching property FK. Soft-delete only (#1) ‚Üí recoverable, and a returned location is revived via `withTrashed()->updateOrCreate`. **Per-agency runs do NOT prune** (`--no-prune` added to `AgencyController` cred-validation syncs + `SyncP24LocationsJob` when agency-scoped) ‚Äî only the authoritative global daily run sweeps. New `--no-prune` flag on the command. Migration `2026_06_26_140000` adds `p24_verified_at` + soft-deletes to `p24_provinces`/`p24_cities` (suburbs already had them from AT-105) + backfills existing rows. Test `P24LocationSweepTest` (healthy run sweeps only unstamped rows / floor skips on a partial run). **FIRST SWEEP DONE on live** (manual run, observed): swept **197 stale cities + 6,108 suburbs** (6,107 stale + the AT-105 phantom); now 9 provinces / 616 cities / 20,754 suburbs active, **0 active rows left unstamped**, **267/267 syndicating listings kept their `p24_suburb_id`**, **0 properties remediated** (nothing depended on a pruned location). All soft-deleted ‚Üí recoverable. **Resilience fix (commit `0df9cf9a`):** the first attempt aborted on a single cURL-28 timeout (P24 slow on one cityId) ‚Äî by design it aborted BEFORE pruning (0 pruned, syndication intact), proving the safety. Every P24 fetch is now wrapped in `fetchRetry` (bounded exponential backoff on transient connection/5xx/429, fail-fast on definitive 4xx, still throws-before-prune if P24 is truly down). Supersedes the AT-105 "AT-106 follow-up" note (reconcile is now obsoleted by the sweep for routine upkeep; keep `p24:reconcile-suburbs` as a manual one-off). The importer page (`/admin/importer/p24-locations`) progress panel now shows a sweep summary on completion ("Swept N stale locations (X cities, Y suburbs) ¬∑ Z properties remediated", or "Sweep skipped ‚Äî tree left intact"). Commits: `ad190521` (sweep) + `cd6890c0` (schema) + `0df9cf9a` (retry) + UI line.

> _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-104 ‚Äî P24 suburb resolution hotfix ‚Üí LIVE (direct to main, no staging)**. Collision suburb names were syndicating to the wrong P24 city ‚Äî South Coast "Glenmore" (Port Edward, p24_id 10790) listings showed as "Durban" (10787). Root cause in `Property24ListingMapper::resolveSuburbId()`: tier 1 checked `pp_suburb_id` (a Private Property column NULL on every CoreX property ‚Üí branch never fired), then fell through to `P24Suburb::lookup()->first()` ‚Äî a bare name match, no city filter ‚Äî picking whichever same-named row sorted first. Fix: trust the stored chain-verified `p24_suburb_id` FK first (fixes 100% of the 265 enabled listings); else name match **disambiguated by city/province**, returned only on a UNIQUE match; else `null` ‚Üí `validate()` skips + flags ("Suburb unmapped ‚Äî manual P24 suburb mapping required"); never a guessed fallback. Removed the name-only `/suburbs/find` auto-resolve + bare fuzzy fallback (could re-introduce the bug; zero enabled props relied on them; `p24:sync-locations` keeps `p24_suburbs` complete). Province text now normalises both sides (P24 stores "KwaZulu Natal", CoreX holds "KwaZulu-Natal"/"KZN"). ## 1. Identity & Stack

**Who:** Johan Reichel (CEO, HFC). Andre Roets (full-stack dev). Two-person team building CoreX OS ‚Äî real estate operating system. HFC (Home Finders Coastal) is the first live agency. Long-term vision: SA's leading real estate OS, replacing PropCon / Sage / Property24 layers across the industry.

**Stack:** Laravel 12 / Blade / Alpine.js. MySQL prod (`hfc_corex`, `hfc_staging`). SQLite local. Vite. Ubuntu on Hetzner `91.99.130.85`. Code at `/corex` (live) and `/corex-staging`. Python AI service `/opt/hf-ai/app.py` port 3100 (not in git).

**Domain:** `corex.hfcoastal.co.za` live. Staging on port 8084.

**Branches:** `main` (live), `Staging`, `HFC2402` (Johan dev), `andre` (Andre dev), feature branches off Staging. Discipline: HFC2402 + andre ‚Üí Staging ‚Üí staging server ‚Üí main ‚Üí live. Hotfix exception: direct to main, then back-sync to Staging.

**VS Code Claude** is the coding agent. Johan pastes prompts, it executes. Specs in `.ai/specs/`, read at start of every prompt.

## 1.5 Operating Principle (read this first, every chat)

CoreX is the best real estate operating system that will ever exist. This is the decision filter for every prompt, every architectural choice, every "should we ship this now" call.

- Best-in-class or rebuild ‚Äî if competitors do something better, we build ours better
- No shortcuts ever ‚Äî later does not exist; build it right the first time
- Integration is the moat ‚Äî every feature seamlessly connects to every other
- Built for agents, not screens ‚Äî we absorb complexity so they don't have to
- AI enhances, never replaces human judgement
- Constraint is fuel ‚Äî build best with what we have, never use lack of resources as an excuse

Decision test before any commit: **does this make CoreX the best, or does it make CoreX merely working?** If the answer is "working", redesign.

"Good enough for now" is never the answer. "We'll fix it later" is never the answer.

See CLAUDE.md "CoreX Operating Principle" section for the full version.

## 2. Working Rules

- **Investigate before fixing.** Every issue: (1) audit, (2) Johan approves fix approach, (3) only then fix prompt. Never guess root causes.
- **One concern per prompt.** Two only if tightly related and same file.
- **Surgical changes.** No refactoring beyond scope.
- **Every prompt opens:** read CLAUDE.md, .ai/STANDARDS.md, relevant spec, and this file.
- **Every prompt closes:** php -l, php artisan view:clear, scripts/dev-check.ps1 if structural change, Tinker verification, **update this CHAT_STARTER.md**.
- **No hard deletes.** SoftDeletes only.
- **PPRA not EAAB. POPIA consent rules apply.**
- **Bug report = code is wrong.** Never blame caching or user error.

### 3.2 IN FLIGHT

- **AT-11 ‚Äî AGENCY BILLING (what agencies pay CoreX)** ‚Äî **Built + 51 tests / 134 assertions green on branch `AT-11-Payment-gate-for-payments`. Not deployed, not promoted.** CoreX charges agencies money and **nothing in the product knew that** ‚Äî no price, no plan, no seat count; the commercial relationship lived entirely outside the system. Two surfaces: **`/corex/billing`** (agency-facing, READ-ONLY ‚Äî an admin sees what they owe *and the itemised arithmetic behind it*, so they can check our maths) and **`/corex/admin/billing`** (owner-only ‚Äî every agency, its seats, plan, list price and payable, with per-agency custom-amount / discount controls). **Pricing (all rates in `config/corex-billing.php` ‚Äî a price change is a config edit, never a code hunt):** *CoreX Team* = flat headcount √ó R450 (‚â§10 users); *CoreX Agency* = R1 495 base + **GRADUATED** seat tiers (1‚Äì10 @R295, 11‚Äì20 @R250, 21+ @R195). The reference case is asserted verbatim in a test: **25 users = 10√ó295 + 10√ó250 + 5√ó195 = R6 425 seats + R1 495 base = R7 920** (a flat 25√óR195 would be R6 370 ‚Äî a R1 550/month error nobody would notice until an agency queried an invoice). Extra branches R750/mo, **first free, charged on BOTH plans** (Johan, 2026-07-14: the plans are two **price shapes, not two feature sets** ‚Äî both get full access to everything; an 8-agent agency with 2 branches is on Team **and** pays for the second branch). **No VAT anywhere** (D4). **Johan's locked decisions:** a billable seat is **ANY active, non-archived user** ‚Äî role is irrelevant, a login is a seat; deactivate someone and they drop off the next bill. Plan **auto-tracks headcount** (11th user ‚Üí Agency) and **every switch emails andre@ + johan@** via the `corex` mailer. **Custom amount and discount are mutually exclusive** ‚Äî the discount comes off the computed price for N months and the agency page shows **"4 months remaining"**. **THE LOAD-BEARING DESIGN: the seat count is COUNTED LIVE on every read, never stored, never incremented** ‚Äî so the bill is right no matter what changed a user (admin screen, bulk import, tinker, raw SQL). Events and the nightly `corex:billing-reconcile` sweep exist **only to make the EMAIL prompt**, never to keep the NUMBER right; a missed event costs a late email, never a wrong invoice. The plan flip is a **compare-and-set** UPDATE, so a page render and the nightly sweep racing the same agency produce **exactly one** email, not two. Discount expiry is **derived arithmetic** (`starts_on + months`), never a stored end-date ‚Äî **no cron can forget to end it**. D5 is guarded three times: UI mode-selector ‚Üí `prohibits`-style validation ‚Üí custom-wins on read, so even a row hand-edited in SQL to hold both yields a correct price instead of double-discounting (asserted). **Owner page is `owner_only` with DELIBERATELY no permission key** ‚Äî a key is *grantable* via Role Manager, and an agency admin handed it would see every competitor's commercial terms (same rationale as Dev Settings / Demo Access); proven by a 403 test. **KNOWN LANDMINE RE-HIT (already logged by AT-230):** a **queued listener on a domain event fatals** ‚Äî `SerializesModels` cannot restore `AbstractDomainEvent`'s parent-declared readonly `$eventId` from the child scope. Listener is therefore **sync**, dispatching `SendAgencyPlanChangedEmail` (a Job carrying **scalars only**) ‚Äî which is the better payload anyway: a job holding an Agency model re-queries it on rehydration, so an agency archived between the switch and the send would `ModelNotFoundException`. **`$queue` is deliberately UNSET** (workers run `queue:work` with no `--queue` flag ‚Üí they drain `default` only; a named queue would strand the email forever). Spec `.ai/specs/agency-billing.md` (¬ß14 records why **nothing** goes in the onboarding wizard: these are CoreX-side commercial terms, not agency-configurable settings ‚Äî putting "your discount %" in a customer's wizard would let them set their own price; **Johan to confirm the omission**). **Phase 2 (NOT built, specced ¬ß13): the payment GATE** ‚Äî AT-11's "cut off / users lock / notifications" ‚Äî will reuse the existing per-agency `maintenance_mode` lockout (AT-93), not a second mechanism; you cannot build a credible gate before the system can say what is owed. New `agency_subscriptions` table (+ migration **backfill** so no pre-existing agency triggers a spurious "switch" email on first reconcile); `schema:dump` re-run **against the test DB**. New perm `billing.view` (admin via all-minus) ‚Üí deploy needs **`corex:sync-permissions --merge-defaults`**. **NEXT:** Johan sign-off on the spec + the wizard omission ‚Üí QA1 deploy ‚Üí Staging.

- **AT-230b ‚Äî Demo connector is UNIVERSAL and UI-CONFIGURED (supersedes the AgencyApiKey wiring below)** ‚Äî **80 tests green, same branch, not deployed.** Johan's call: the demo already exists and has a System Owner login, so the connection should be set up **in the browser**, and the credential should be **one universal connector, not a per-agency key** (there is only ever one demo agency). Replaced the two `AgencyApiKey` demo scopes with **`demo_connectors` + `DemoConnector` + `demo.connector` middleware** ‚Äî an `AgencyApiKey` is *agency-scoped* (it resolves an agency as the tenant for `AgencyScope`), but demo grants are RR Technologies' **sales** data, not tenant data; pinning them to an arbitrary agency was a lie in the data model AND put a grantable `demo:*` scope in the per-agency key UI. Token = `cx_demo_xxxxxxxx.<48ch>`, sha256 at rest, shown once; **rotation is INSERT + revoke-the-old** (so the table is also the audit trail of every credential the demo has held, and a rotated-out token stops working immediately ‚Äî a rotation that left the old one live would be worthless against a leak). **LIVE:** Dev Settings ‚Üí Demo Access ‚Üí **Demo connection** (issue / replace / revoke; `last_used_at` shown ‚Äî *"Never"* is the key diagnostic, separating "the demo isn't calling us" from "it's calling and being refused"). **DEMO:** Dev Settings ‚Üí **Demo Connection** ‚Äî paste the CoreX address + token, **Test connection** (`GET /api/v1/demo-access/ping`); the URL is stored plain and the **token encrypted** (`Crypt::encryptString` ‚Äî it must be replayable so it can't be hashed, and the demo box is disposable). **A blank token field means "keep it", not "clear it"** (the secret is never rendered back, so blank-as-clear would wipe it whenever someone edited only the URL). **THE TWO ESCAPE HATCHES that make UI config safe:** the gate fails closed, so a bad token would otherwise brick the demo ‚Äî the connection would be its own prerequisite. So (1) **`demo-owner-login` is exempt from the gate** (safe: it is password-protected AND refuses non-owners ‚Äî a password-protected login page being public is not a leak), and (2) **a signed-in System Owner bypasses the gate on a LOCAL role check** that never consults primary, so it holds exactly when primary is unreachable. **What is NOT exempt: `demo-login/{role}`** ‚Äî the *passwordless* role login, the actual door prospects walk through; it is gated by `EnsureDemoGrant` and re-checked in the controller. **BUG FIXED: `DemoLoginController::isEnabled()` required `!environment('production')` ‚Äî but the demo host RUNS `APP_ENV=production`, so every demo-mode surface, including the System Owner login, silently 404'd on the very box they exist for.** Now gates on `Instance::isDemo()`. Deploy ordering is now **soft**: flipping the role early no longer locks anyone out, because the owner can still sign in and finish the wiring. Spec ¬ß5.1/¬ß5.2/¬ß15 rewritten.

- **AT-230 ‚Äî Demo Access Control** ‚Äî **Built + 58 tests green on branch `AT-147-Demo-mode-hide` (not promoted, not deployed).** Time-boxed, company-attributed, emailed credentials gating `demo1.corexos.co.za`: clickwrap T&C, session + page-view telemetry, per-company watermark, 3-day reset countdown, owner-only admin UI under Dev Settings. **‚öÝÔ∏è THE SPEC DID NOT EXIST** ‚Äî `.ai/specs/demo-access-control.md` was absent from the repo and from every git ref; it was **authored here from the build prompt + codebase investigation, and its ¬ß0 lists the 12 contracts Claude invented. Johan must review ¬ß0** (notably: archive uses an explicit `archived_at` column, **not** `SoftDeletes`, because a global scope hiding rows is wrong for an evidence table). **One codebase, two instance roles:** new `COREX_INSTANCE_ROLE` (`primary`|`demo`) + `App\Support\Instance`. Durable records (5 tables: grants, T&C versions, acceptances, sessions, page views) live on **primary**, because the demo DB is destroyed every 3 days. Demo‚Üíprimary over the EXISTING `agency-api` guard (2 new `AgencyApiKey` scopes `demo:gate`/`demo:telemetry`) at **`/api/v1/demo-access/*`** ‚Äî NOT `/api/v1/demo/*`, which is already the mobile app's group. **Load-bearing invariants (each has a test):** grant `status` is DERIVED never stored; `expires_at` is **NULL until first login and NULL is NOT expired**; first-login stamping is a conditional `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ WHERE first_login_at IS NULL` (two tabs = exactly one winner, no silent trial extension); T&C versions are **immutable** (edit = publish v2; v1 acceptances still render v1 text); the **gate fails CLOSED, telemetry fails OPEN**; next-reset is a **pure function of time** (anchor + 3n days @ 03:00 SAST) so the banner and the scheduler cannot disagree; revoke bites within the 60s cache TTL and the confirm dialog **says so**. **THREE REAL BUGS the tests caught:** (1) a queued listener on a domain event **fatals** ‚Äî `SerializesModels` cannot restore `AbstractDomainEvent`'s parent-declared readonly `$eventId` from the child scope; the listener is now sync and the *Mailable* carries `ShouldQueue`. (2) `$middleware->web(append:)` is **not enough** to run before `auth` ‚Äî Laravel's priority list hoists `Authenticate`, so an unauthenticated visitor hit `/login` (which on demo renders the demo-role buttons) **without passing the gate**; fixed with `prependToPriorityList(before: AuthenticatesRequests::class)` ‚Äî note the anchor is the **contract**, not `Authenticate::class`, which silently matches nothing. (3) the watermark had to go in **BOTH** `corex-app.blade.php` (~159 views) **and** `corex.blade.php` (~231 views) ‚Äî the docs point only at the first, which would leave the majority of pages unmarked. Owner-only via `owner_only`, **zero permission keys** (`corex:sync-permissions` = 0 created/0 updated ‚Äî a key is *grantable*, and one Role-Manager mis-click would show an agency admin its competitors). `DemoTncVersionSeeder` (v1) registered in `deploy:sync-reference-data` ‚Äî without v1 the clickwrap has nothing to show and **every prospect is hard-blocked**. Shared sandbox + 3-day reset are **Johan's accepted decisions (2026-07-11)**, not compromises. **Deploy ordering that will bite (spec ¬ß15): primary must be deployed and the AgencyApiKey minted BEFORE a host is flipped to `COREX_INSTANCE_ROLE=demo`** ‚Äî otherwise the gate correctly fails closed and locks everyone out. 5 test files, 58 tests / 197 assertions.

Tests `tests/Feature/Properties/PropertyIndexSyndicationControlTest.php` 6/6 (incl. a show-page regression pinning the extraction). No migration, no new permission key.

Also fixed the **same cross-agency template leak** in `PropertyMarketingController@index` (was `->where(user_id)->orWhere(is_global)`). **To run it locally you must set `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` in `.env`** (it's empty); it works on staging/prod where the key is set.
